msg:I am a frequent visitor to Wuzhen. I have stayed in B&Bs and Alila. This time it is a designer-themed hotel that was bought during Double Eleven. It is not unusual in Wuzhen where B&Bs are everywhere, but the simple black decoration is still very eye-catching. .

Now that Iâ€™ve finished talking about the advantages, letâ€™s start talking about why I only gave it 1 star.

1-The room is small

The order stated 25-30 square meters. I also looked at the review pictures and thought it should be good, but in fact, the room was very small! There is a double bed, a bay window and the rest is the toilet.
The toilet faces the window, which is very uncomfortable. I think it may be because of the coupons that the room given to me is small, which is understandable. But at the same price, I believe you can definitely find bigger and better hotels/B&Bs in Wuzhen!

2- Room smell

There was an indescribable smell as soon as I entered the room. I initially thought it was the smell of dust from not opening the window for a long time. Until the air conditioner was turned on, a smell of toilet sewers hit my face. This was one of the reasons why I didn't sleep well at night. Later, I Only then did we realize that their toilet was directly opposite our window.

3- Room air conditioner

The air conditioner in the room was unusually loud. I saw other guests mention this in their reviews, but because it was minus 7 degrees Celsius when I went there, I had already opened the window due to the smell in the room. It was unrealistic not to turn on the air conditioner! This is also the direct reason why I didnâ€™t sleep well all night!

4- The bathroom water is small

The bath water in the bathroom is very small. It is unrealistic to take a warm bath in such a cold weather! Shivering from the cold! I really canâ€™t believe how old the facilities are in a modern hotel!

5- Chris**as music

It was Chris**as when I went there, and the same song started to play from 9 a.m. to the evening. Two large speakers were placed next to the hotel room, and they continued to play! You can hear it clearly even if the window is closed in the room. It wasn't until we returned to the hotel in the evening that we couldn't bear it anymore and asked to close it.

6- Breakfast

The climax came. Breakfast was a set menu, but I ate unidentified hairs. The male waiter who made our coffee went to smoke nearby. We called another waitress at the bar and showed her the poached eggs with hairs and they were not. Floating on top, it's really inside the egg whites of fried poached eggs. The waitress didn't even say sorry, she just told me that she would tell the kitchen! Excuse me? I'm not asking you to compensate. The simplest sentence is "I'm sorry. Is it worth it?" I am simply speechless!

Before we left and checked out, the front desk asked us how our stay was, and we could only say lightly that it was not as good as we imagined!
